{

    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;

    u_xlat0 = u_xlat26.xxyy * u_xlat0.xyxy + vs_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat26.xy = u_xlat0.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat26.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat26.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat26.xy = u_xlat5.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat26.xy = u_xlat26.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat5.x = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat26.xy = u_xlat26.xy * u_xlat5.xx;
    u_xlat26.xy = u_xlat26.xy * vec2(vec2(_Maskadjust, _Maskadjust));
    u_xlat10_5.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat26.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat26.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat26.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = log2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_3.www * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(5.0, 5.0, 5.0) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat46) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat46) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb39 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb39) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_14 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_14 = min(u_xlat16_14, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_14 * u_xlat16_1.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat39 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat7.xy = vec2(u_xlat39) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat7.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat10_39 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat10_39 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat39 = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat15.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat44 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat44);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat44) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat15.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat44 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat44);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat44) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xy = u_xlat16_5.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat16_5.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyw;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);

    u_xlat16_42 = max(u_xlat16_42, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_47 = (-u_xlat16_42) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_47 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat16_47;

    u_xlat2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat2.x;

    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_3.x + _MetallicOffset;

    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_20) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_42) + u_xlat16_20;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec4 u_xlat1;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_46 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_46;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb47 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb47 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb6 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb6 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlatb47 || u_xlatb6;
    u_xlat16_45 = (u_xlatb47) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_46 * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat48 = inversesqrt(u_xlat48);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat48) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat48 = min(max(u_xlat48, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat48 = clamp(u_xlat48, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_50 = abs(u_xlat16_50) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_50 = min(u_xlat16_50, 1.0);
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat35;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_50) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat15.zxy) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat35) * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.zxy) * u_xlat9.yzx;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * u_xlat9.zxy + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat35) * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.y = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.z = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);

    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_46 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_46;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb47 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb47 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb6 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb6 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlatb47 || u_xlatb6;
    u_xlat16_45 = (u_xlatb47) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_46 * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat48 = inversesqrt(u_xlat48);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat48) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat48 = min(max(u_xlat48, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat48 = clamp(u_xlat48, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_50 = abs(u_xlat16_50) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_50 = min(u_xlat16_50, 1.0);
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat35;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat16_52 = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 + u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_52)) + (-u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_50) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_53 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_53 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_53;
    u_xlat16_53 = u_xlat16_53 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_9 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat16_53);
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_9.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_11.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = max(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_11.x = log2(u_xlat16_11.x);
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_46 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_46;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb47 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb47 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb6 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb6 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlatb47 || u_xlatb6;
    u_xlat16_45 = (u_xlatb47) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_46 * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat48 = inversesqrt(u_xlat48);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat48) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat48 = min(max(u_xlat48, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat48 = clamp(u_xlat48, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_50 = abs(u_xlat16_50) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_50 = min(u_xlat16_50, 1.0);
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat35;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_50) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat15.zxy) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat35) * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.zxy) * u_xlat9.yzx;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * u_xlat9.zxy + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat35) * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.y = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.z = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.xy = vec2(u_xlat35) * u_xlat9.xy;
    u_xlat9.xy = u_xlat9.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_12.x;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiHighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiST1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DigiPow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _DigiDistore;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

float u_xlat19;

float u_xlat28;
int u_xlati28;
bool u_xlatb28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat35;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
bool u_xlatb42;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;

mediump float u_xlat16_46;
float u_xlat47;
bool u_xlatb47;
float u_xlat48;
float u_xlat49;
mediump float u_xlat16_50;
mediump float u_xlat16_52;
mediump float u_xlat16_53;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_46 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_46;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb47 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb47 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb6 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb6 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlatb47 || u_xlatb6;
    u_xlat16_45 = (u_xlatb47) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_46 * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat48 = inversesqrt(u_xlat48);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat48) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat48 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat48 = min(max(u_xlat48, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat48 = clamp(u_xlat48, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_50 = abs(u_xlat16_50) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_50 = min(u_xlat16_50, 1.0);
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat35;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat35);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;

    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;

    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_45) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat49 = inversesqrt(u_xlat49);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_46 = abs(u_xlat16_46) + 0.00400000019;

    u_xlat50 = min(max(u_xlat50, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8.x = min(max(u_xlat8.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8.x = clamp(u_xlat8.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat22 * 0.125 + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat16_48 = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 + u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_48)) + (-u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat22 * u_xlat22;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_52 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_9.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_52 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_52 + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_52);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45 + 1.0;
    u_xlat36 = float(1.0) / u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat12.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_48) * u_xlat12.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat50) * u_xlat50 + 1.0;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat50;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_45 / u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_2.z * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat5.x = min(u_xlat5.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat49);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = _SHshadow + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_48 = log2(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * _AddlightScale;
    u_xlat16_48 = exp2(u_xlat16_48);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_52 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_52 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_52);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_52);
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) * u_xlat16_4.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_45 / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_48) * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(vec3(_AddlightLerp, _AddlightLerp, _AddlightLerp)) + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_2.z + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat22 * u_xlat16_16 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat22 / u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);

    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;

    u_xlat16_44 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_44 * u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_16 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_13.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));

        u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat47) * u_xlat5.xyz;
        u_xlat47 = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
        u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).x + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).y;
        u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat47;
        u_xlat16_30 = dot(_AdditionalLightsSpotDirDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).w;
        u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30;
        u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_30;
        u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).xyz;
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    }
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(_Gspeed) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat5.y = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.xxyy * u_xlat5.xyxy + vs_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat0.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat5.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat28 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat28) * u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_Maskadjust, _Maskadjust));
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = log2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(5.0, 5.0, 5.0) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlatb42 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb42) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat42 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat10_42 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_16 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = min(u_xlat16_16, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_2.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat10_42 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = log2(u_xlat16_46);
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat1.x = exp2(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat1.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat42) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;

out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat10_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat10_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat10_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
vec3 u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
float u_xlat14;
uint u_xlatu14;
vec3 u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
float u_xlat19;
float u_xlat22;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_24;
float u_xlat28;
int u_xlati28;
bool u_xlatb28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat36;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
bool u_xlatb42;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
float u_xlat47;
mediump float u_xlat16_48;
float u_xlat49;
float u_xlat50;
mediump float u_xlat16_52;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_45) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat49 = inversesqrt(u_xlat49);

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat10_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat10_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat10_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat10_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_45) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat10_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat49 = inversesqrt(u_xlat49);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_46 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_46 = abs(u_xlat16_46) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_46 = min(u_xlat16_46, 1.0);
    u_xlat50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat50 = clamp(u_xlat50, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat22 * 0.125 + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;

    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat22 + 0.125;

    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat22 * u_xlat22;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;

    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.zxy) * u_xlat9.yzx;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * u_xlat9.zxy + (-u_xlat11.xyz);

    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.y = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.z = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.xy = vec2(u_xlat36) * u_xlat9.xy;
    u_xlat9.xy = u_xlat9.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_52 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_9.xyz = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat9.xy, u_xlat16_52).xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat10_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45 + 1.0;
    u_xlat36 = float(1.0) / u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_48) * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat50) * u_xlat50 + 1.0;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat50;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_45 / u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_2.z * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat5.x = min(u_xlat5.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat11.xyz;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;

layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_24;
float u_xlat28;
int u_xlati28;
bool u_xlatb28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat36;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
bool u_xlatb42;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
float u_xlat47;
mediump float u_xlat16_48;
