mediump float u_xlat16_52;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_16) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_45 = (-u_xlat16_45) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat49 = inversesqrt(u_xlat49);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_46 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_46 = abs(u_xlat16_46) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_46 = min(u_xlat16_46, 1.0);
    u_xlat50 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat50 = min(max(u_xlat50, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat50 = clamp(u_xlat50, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8.x = min(max(u_xlat8.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8.x = clamp(u_xlat8.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat22 * 0.125 + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_24.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_24.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = (-u_xlat16_46) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat22 * u_xlat22;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat15.zxy) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.zxy) * u_xlat9.yzx;
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat15.yzx) * u_xlat9.zxy + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.y = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.z = dot((-u_xlat15.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat9.xy = vec2(u_xlat36) * u_xlat9.xy;
    u_xlat9.xy = u_xlat9.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_52 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_52;
    u_xlat16_52 = u_xlat16_52 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat9.xy, u_xlat16_52).xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45 + 1.0;
    u_xlat36 = float(1.0) / u_xlat36;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_48) * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat50) * u_xlat50 + 1.0;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat50;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_45 / u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_2.z * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat5.x = min(u_xlat5.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat49) * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat49);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = _SHshadow + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_48 = log2(u_xlat16_16);

    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec2 u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
vec3 u_xlat14;
bool u_xlatb14;
float u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_25;
vec2 u_xlat28;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat32;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
bool u_xlatb42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_48;
float u_xlat50;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_16 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat14.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat14.zxy) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat43);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat43) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat14.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat14.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat43);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat43) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_30.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyw = u_xlat16_30.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyw = u_xlat16_30.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyw;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyw;
    u_xlat16_30.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_30.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_30.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_30.x = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_30.x = max(u_xlat16_30.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_30.x = min(u_xlat16_30.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_44 = (-u_xlat16_30.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * u_xlat16_30.x;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat1.xy, u_xlat16_44).xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_30.x * u_xlat16_30.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_44 * u_xlat16_44 + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_48 = (-u_xlat16_45) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_45 = min(max(u_xlat16_45, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_45 = clamp(u_xlat16_45, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_48 = (-u_xlat16_48) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = (-u_xlat16_30.x) + u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_48 = min(max(u_xlat16_48, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_48 = clamp(u_xlat16_48, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_45) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_48) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = abs(u_xlat16_45) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_45 = min(u_xlat16_45, 1.0);
    u_xlat43 = (-u_xlat16_45) + 1.0;
    u_xlat4.x = log2(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat4.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat4.x = exp2(u_xlat4.x);
    u_xlat4.x = (-u_xlat4.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat43 * u_xlat43;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_6.y * u_xlat16_6.y;
    u_xlat50 = u_xlat16_6.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat18.x * 0.125 + u_xlat50;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat18.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat50);
    u_xlat10.y = u_xlat18.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat9.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_11.xy = max(u_xlat10.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_11.xy = u_xlat16_11.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_25.xyz = u_xlat16_11.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_25.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_4.z));
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_45 = exp2(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_45 = min(u_xlat16_45, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat50 = dot(u_xlat18.xyz, u_xlat18.xyz);
    u_xlat50 = inversesqrt(u_xlat50);
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * vec3(u_xlat50);
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat18.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18.x = min(max(u_xlat18.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18.x = clamp(u_xlat18.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat32 = (-u_xlat18.x) * u_xlat18.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_44 * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat18.x * u_xlat18.x + u_xlat32;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_44 / u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat16_30.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat18.z = u_xlat16_30.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xz = u_xlat18.xz * u_xlat18.xz;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat18.x * u_xlat32;
    u_xlat18.x = min(u_xlat18.x, 100.0);

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
float u_xlat13;
bool u_xlatb13;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_20;
float u_xlat21;
float u_xlat22;
vec2 u_xlat26;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat39;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
bool u_xlatb39;
float u_xlat40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
mediump float u_xlat16_43;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
float u_xlat47;
float u_xlat48;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb13 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb13 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb13 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_28.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_28.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_28.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_28.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat26.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat13;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat13);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat26.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_28.xy = u_xlat16_28.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_28.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_28.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_28.x = u_xlat16_28.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_28.x = exp2(u_xlat16_28.x);
    u_xlat16_28.x = min(u_xlat16_28.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_28.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_41 = max(u_xlat16_41, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_41 = min(u_xlat16_41, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_42 = (-u_xlat16_41) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_43 = u_xlat16_43 + u_xlat16_43;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_43)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_6.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_42 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_42 = max(u_xlat16_42, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_42 = log2(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_42 = exp2(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_28.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat26.x = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat16_42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat26.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat26.x;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat26.xxx;
    u_xlat16_43 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_43) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_43 = u_xlat16_43;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.zw = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec2 u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
vec3 u_xlat14;
bool u_xlatb14;
float u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_25;
vec2 u_xlat28;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat32;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
bool u_xlatb42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_48;
float u_xlat50;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_16 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_16;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat14.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat14.zxy) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat43);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat43) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat14.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat14.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat43);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat43) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_30.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyw = u_xlat16_30.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyw = u_xlat16_30.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyw;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyw;
    u_xlat16_30.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_30.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_30.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_30.x = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_30.x = max(u_xlat16_30.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_30.x = min(u_xlat16_30.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_44 = (-u_xlat16_30.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;

    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat28.xy = u_xlat28.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat1.x = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat28.xy = u_xlat28.xy * u_xlat1.xx;
    u_xlat28.xy = u_xlat28.xy * vec2(vec2(_Maskadjust, _Maskadjust));
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat28.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat28.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat28.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_FurTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = log2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_5.www * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(5.0, 5.0, 5.0) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat4.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat4.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb42 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb42) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_16 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = min(u_xlat16_16, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_2.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat42 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat10_42 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat4.xy).x;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat10_42 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat42) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

{

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;

#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OutlineWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Offset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _FarWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _NearWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _color1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScreenResolution;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _OutlineMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump float vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat9;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = max(u_xlat9, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(_lightDir.xyz, _lightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * _lightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-_OutlineColor.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz + _OutlineColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = textureLod(_OutlineMap, in_TEXCOORD0.xy, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat1.w * abs(_Offset);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat3.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].xy * u_xlat3.xx + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].xy * u_xlat3.zz + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat3.xy, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat9) * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy / _ScreenParams.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _ScreenResolution.yy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat1.y * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].w;
    u_xlat9 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].w * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat9;
    u_xlat9 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].w * u_xlat1.z + u_xlat9;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat9 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3].w;
    u_xlat0.yz = vec2(u_xlat9) * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.150000006, 0.00462962966, 0.00462962966);
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat0.yz / u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].xyz * u_xlat1.zzz + u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat3.xy + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat3.xy, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.x = sqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.x = max(u_xlat3.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat3.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 100.0;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz / abs(u_xlat3.zzz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].z;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].z;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].z;
    u_xlat1.w = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].z;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    gl_Position.z = dot(u_xlat1, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].x;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].x;
    gl_Position.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].y;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].y;
    gl_Position.y = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.yzw);
    u_xlat0.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].w;
    u_xlat0.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].w;
    gl_Position.w = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.zw);
    return;
}

#endif

    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyw = in_TEXCOORD0.xyy;
    vs_TEXCOORD2 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScreenResolution;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _DigiST1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DigiChange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiHighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _DigiScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_3;
bool u_xlatb9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w * vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _DigiChange;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = (-_DigiBaseColor0) + _DigiBaseColor1;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1.xxxx * u_xlat16_2 + _DigiBaseColor0;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = texture(_ClothTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xy;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_10 = (u_xlatb9) ? u_xlat0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiChange + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _DigiHighColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}
